[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation**: The problematic buffer was allocated through:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `xmlCreateEntity` → `xmlStrdup` → `xmlStrndup` → `xmlFuzzMalloc` → `malloc`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The allocation created a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte region at address `[0m[1;36m0x502000000b30[0m[39m`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The entity was added via `xmlAddEntity` and `xmlSAX2EntityDecl`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Overflow Characteristics**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Attempted to read [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes starting at address `[0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[39m`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This address is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte allocated region [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x502000000b30[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0x502000000b37[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The read operation extends [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m bytes beyond the valid buffer[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entity Processing Context**: The vulnerability occurs specifically during [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity declaration processing in the DTD [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocument Type Definition[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m internal [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubset, suggesting issues with entity value expansion involving parameter entities [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mPEs[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Management**: The buffer allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m appears insufficient for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe subsequent copy operation [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating either:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Incorrect size calculation during allocation[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Missing bounds checking before the copy operation[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Incorrect assumptions about entity value length[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Stack Trace Consistency**: Both the allocation and overflow stack traces show [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsistent processing through the entity declaration and parsing infrastructure[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas Requiring Investigation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m484[0m[39m:     * Add extra cost and some fixed cost.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m485[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m486[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlSaturatedAdd[0m[1;39m([0m[39mexpandedSize, extra[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m487[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mxmlSaturatedAdd[0m[1;39m([0m[39mexpandedSize, XML_ENT_FIXED_COST[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m488[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m489[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m490[0m[39m:     * It's important to always use saturation arithmetic when tracking[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m491[0m[39m:     * entity sizes to make the size checks reliable. If [0m[32m"sizeentcopy"[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m492[0m[39m:     * overflows, we have to abort.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m493[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m494[0m[39m:    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*expandedSize > XML_PARSER_ALLOWED_EXPANSION[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m &&[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m495[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*expandedSize >= ULONG_MAX[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m496[0m[39m:         [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*expandedSize [0m[35m/[0m[39m ctxt->maxAmpl > consumed[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m497[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlFatalErrMsg[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, XML_ERR_RESOURCE_LIMIT,[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m498[0m[39m:                       [0m[32m"Maximum entity amplification factor exceeded, see "[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m499[0m[39m:                       [0m[32m"xmlCtxtSetMaxAmplification.\n"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m500[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mxmlHaltParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m501[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m502[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m503[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m504[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m505[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Vulnerability[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I've identified the root [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `parser.[0m[1;92mc:4005[0m[39m` in the `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` function[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: The code incorrectly pairs `ent->name` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpointer to entity name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith `ent->length` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength of entity content[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, causing a type mismatch where memcpy[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempts to read [0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes from a [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The Bug**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m LINE [0m[1;36m4005[0m[39m - INCORRECT[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis tries to copy `ent->length` bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m48[0m[39m bytes - the content length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m from [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ent->name` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m7[0m[39m bytes - the name string [0m[32m"entity1"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, resulting in reading [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m bytes [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the allocated buffer.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Core Insights from Code Analysis[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entity Structure** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mentities.h:[0m[1;36m42[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m65[0m[39m, entities.[0m[1;92mc:119[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m170[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ent->name`: Contains the entity's name [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"entity1"[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ent->content`: Contains the entity's value/content[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ent->length`: Contains the length of `ent->content` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNOT the name[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct Usage Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:3988[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4378[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4627[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All correct usages pair `ent->content` with `ent->length`[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Example: `[0m[1;35mxmlExpandPEsInEntityValue[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, buf, ent->content, ent->length, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **When to Use Entity Name** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:4646[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When outputting entity reference: `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddString[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&buf, ent->name, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Must use `[0m[1;35mxmlStrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to get the name's actual length[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **The [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m Pattern** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mparser.[0m[1;92mc:3993[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m4007[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is a non-standard pattern handling [0m[32m"*%name;"[0m[39m sequences[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Intended to add entity content directly without recursive expansion[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Unlike the standard [0m[32m"%"[0m[39m pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3950[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3992[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which recursively expands [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Missing entity expansion checks [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXML_ENT_EXPANDING flag, xmlParserEntityCheck[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Correct the Type Mismatch[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `parser.c`[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line**: [0m[1;36m4005[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->name, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mxmlSBufAddEntitySecure[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Semantic Correctness**: The function `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` is designed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto expand parameter entities by replacing entity references with their content, not[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir names.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Consistency with Codebase**: This matches the pattern used throughout libxml2:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m3988[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mxmlExpandPEsInEntityValue[0m[1;39m([0m[39mctxt, buf, ent->content, ent->length, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m4378[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbuf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Line [0m[1;36m4627[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mxmlSBufAddString[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&buf, ent->content, ent->length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type Safety**: The `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` function signature expects:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parameter [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Pointer to string data to copy[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parameter [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Length of that string data[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using `ent->content` with `ent->length` satisfies this contract[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Security Design**: The `xmlSBufAddEntitySecure` function is designed to safely[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandle entity content expansion with buffer overflow protection. It expects the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer and length to match.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m pattern appears to be a special case for [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirect content insertion without recursive expansion [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlike the standard [0m[32m"%"[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Changing to `ent->content` preserves this semantic while fixing the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer overflow.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Additional Safety Consideration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional Enhancement[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhile not strictly required to fix the immediate vulnerability, consider adding a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull check for `ent->content` before the call, similar to the standard [0m[32m"%"[0m[39m case at [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m3960[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3976[0m[39m:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39ment->content == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Handle case where content is not loaded[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Similar to lines [0m[1;36m3960[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3976[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    return;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHowever, since this is the [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m pattern and might have different semantics, this [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menhancement should only be added if it doesn't break the intended functionality.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Single line modification that directly addresses the root [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcause[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: Does not modify the fuzzing harness, test code, or [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal APIs[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type Correct**: Properly pairs data pointer with its corresponding length[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Pattern Consistent**: Follows the established pattern throughout the codebase[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Security Preserving**: Maintains the security design of [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlSBufAddEntitySecure`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: The change is localized to the buggy line and doesn't [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffect other code paths[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: If the [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m pattern was intentionally designed to output entity [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich seems unlikely given the context[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this fix would change that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: The analysis strongly suggests this is a bug, not intentional [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesign:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No documentation supports [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m as a valid XML pattern[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The comment at line [0m[1;36m4003[0m[39m says [0m[32m"Grow the buffer to handle the input"[0m[39m suggesting [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontent expansion[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function name `xmlExpandPEsInEntityValue` implies expanding entity values [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not names[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No test cases in the codebase use the [0m[32m"*%"[0m[39m pattern[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Confidence**: Very high that this is a bug fix, not a behavior change.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
